Jett, Jr.\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Steven_MacLean_(astronaut)" title="Steven MacLean (astronaut)">\n          Steven MacLean\n         </a>\n         <div class="" style="width:100%; text-align:center; border-top:1px #aaa solid">\n          <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_program" title="Space Shuttle program">\n           Space Shuttle program\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <div style="width:100%">\n          <div class="noprint" style="float: left; text-align:left;padding-right:0.5em;">\n           \xe2\x86\x90\n           <a href="/wiki/STS-121" title="STS-121">\n            STS-121\n           </a>\n          </div>\n          <div class="noprint" style="float: right; text-align:right;padding-left:0.5em;">\n           <a href="/wiki/STS-116" title="STS-116">\n            STS-116\n           </a>\n           \xe2\x86\x92\n          </div>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        STS-115\n       </b>\n       was a\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n        Space Shuttle\n       </a>\n       mission to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS) flown by\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">\n        Space Shuttle\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       . It was the first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS_assembly_sequence" title="ISS assembly sequence">\n        assembly mission\n       </a>\n       to the ISS after the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Columbia disaster">\n        <i>\n         Columbia\n        </i>\n        disaster\n       </a>\n       , following the two successful\n       <i>\n        Return to Flight\n       </i>\n       missions,\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-114" title="STS-114">\n        STS-114\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-121" title="STS-121">\n        STS-121\n       </a>\n       . STS-115 launched from\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center_Launch_Complex_39" title="Kennedy Space Center Launch Complex 39">\n        Pad 39-B\n       </a>\n       at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       on 9 September 2006 at 11:14:55\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone_(North_America)" title="Eastern Time Zone (North America)">\n        EDT\n       </a>\n       (15:14:55\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The mission is also referred to as\n       <b>\n        ISS-12A\n       </b>\n       by the ISS program. The mission delivered the second port-side\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        truss\n       </a>\n       segment (ITS P3/P4), a pair of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS_Solar_Arrays" title="ISS Solar Arrays">\n        solar arrays\n       </a>\n       (2A and 4A), and\n       <a href="/wiki/Battery_(electricity)" title="Battery (electricity)">\n        batteries\n       </a>\n       . A total of three spacewalks were performed, during which the crew connected the systems on the installed trusses, prepared them for deployment, and did other maintenance work on the station.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       STS-115 was originally scheduled to launch in April 2003. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Columbia disaster">\n        <i>\n         Columbia\n        </i>\n        accident\n       </a>\n       in February 2003 pushed the date back to 27 August 2006, which was again moved back for various reasons, including a threat from\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ernesto_(2006)" title="Hurricane Ernesto (2006)">\n        Tropical Storm Ernesto\n       </a>\n       and the strongest lightning strike to ever hit an occupied shuttle launchpad.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#Crew">\n Tanner\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         Fourth spaceflight\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Mission Specialist 4\n        </th>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <span class="flagicon">\n          <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n           <img alt="United States" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>\n          </a>\n         </span>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heidemarie_M._Stefanyshyn-Piper" title="Heidemarie M. Stefanyshyn-Piper">\n          Heidemarie M. Stefanyshyn-Piper\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         First spaceflight\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <small>\n        Note:The P3/P4 Truss segment and batteries were so heavy (more than 17.5\n        <a href="/wiki/Short_ton" title="Short ton">\n         short tons\n        </a>\n        , or roughly 16\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Metric_ton" title="Metric ton">\n         metric tons\n        </a>\n        ) that the crew count was reduced from seven to six.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">\n         <a href="#cite_note-2">\n          [2]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </small>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Crew_notes">\n        Crew notes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-115&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Crew notes">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Canadian Space Agency astronaut MacLean became the first Canadian to operate\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       and its Mobile Base in space as he was handed a new set of solar arrays from Ferguson and Burbank controlling the original Canadian robotic arm, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        Canadarm\n       </a>\n       . MacLean performed a spacewalk, becoming only the second Canadian, after\n       <a href="/wiki/Chris_Hadfield" title="Chris Hadfield">\n        Chris Hadfield\n       </a>\n       to do so.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The mission patch worn on the clothing used by the astronauts of STS-115 was designed by Graham Huber, Peter Hui, and Gigi Lui, three students at\n       <a href="/wiki/York_University" title="York University">\n        York University\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">\n        Toronto, Ontario\n       </a>\n       , the same university that Steve MacLean attended. The students also designed Steve MacLean\'s personal patch for this mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_payloads">\n        Mission payloads\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-115&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Mission payloads">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The primary payload was the second left-side\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        ITS P3/P4 Truss\n       </a>\n       segment, a pair of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS_Solar_Arrays" title="ISS Solar Arrays">\n        solar arrays\n       </a>\n       , and associated batteries.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_objectives">\n        Mission objectives\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-115&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Mission objectives">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Delivery and installation of two truss segments (P3 and P4)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Delivery and deployment of two new solar arrays (4A and 2A)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Perform three spacewalks to connect truss segments, remove restraints on solar arrays, and prepare the station for the next assembly mission by\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-116" title="STS-116">\n         STS-116\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_background">\n        Mission background\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-115&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Mission background">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       NASA managers decided to move the STS-115 launch date forward to 27 August to obtain better lighting conditions to photograph the external tank. This occurred before with\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-31" title="STS-31">\n        STS-31\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-82" title="STS-82">\n        STS-82\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The launch window was co-ordinated with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_TMA-9" title="Soyuz TMA-9">\n        Soyuz TMA-9\n       </a>\n       launch in mid-September, which delivered a new ISS crew and fresh supplies to the station. The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soyuz_spacecraft" title="Soyuz spacecraft">\n        Soyuz spacecraft\n       </a>\n       operationally did not dock to the station while the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n        Space Shuttle\n       </a>\n       was there.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The mission marks:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ql_1-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ql-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        147th NASA manned space flight.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        116th space shuttle flight since\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-1" title="STS-1">\n         STS-1\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        27th flight of\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        91st post-\n        <i>\n         Challenger\n        </i>\n        mission.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        3rd post-\n        <i>\n         Columbia\n        </i>\n        mission.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        1st post-\n        <i>\n         Columbia\n        </i>\n        mission of\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n        .\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Launch_preparations">\n        Launch preparations\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-115&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Launch preparations">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rollover_Atlantis.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2246" data-file-width="3000" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Rollover_Atlantis.jpg/220px-Rollover_Atlantis.jpg"
